\DoxyCodeLine{03158\ \textcolor{comment}{/**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03159\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Computes\ the\ integer\ square\ root}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03160\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ @remarks\ The\ calculation\ is\ performed\ using\ an\ algorithm\ which\ iterates\ through\ each\ binary\ digit\ of\ the\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ and\ tests\ whether\ setting\ that\ digit\ to\ 1\ would\ cause\ the\ square\ of\ the\ value\ to\ be\ greater\ than\ the\ argument}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ value.\ The\ algorithm\ is\ described\ in\ detail\ here:\ http://ww1.microchip.com/downloads/en/AppNotes/91040a.pdf\ .}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03163\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03674\ \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/\ double\ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03675\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03676\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Clang\ 3.5\ in\ the\ iOS\ toolchain\ has\ an\ ICE\ triggered\ by\ NEON\ intrisics\ for\ double.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03677\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Confirmed\ at\ least\ with\ \_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_\ =\ 6000054.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03678\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ \_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03679\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Let's\ hope\ that\ by\ the\ time\ \_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_\ hits\ the\ 601*\ range,\ the\ bug\ will\ be\ fixed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03680\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ https://gist.github.com/yamaya/2924292\ suggests\ that\ the\ 3\ first\ digits\ are\ only\ updated\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03681\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ major\ toolchain\ updates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03682\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ EIGEN\_APPLE\_DOUBLE\_NEON\_BUG\ (\_\_apple\_build\_version\_\_\ <\ 6010000)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03683\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03684\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ EIGEN\_APPLE\_DOUBLE\_NEON\_BUG\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03685\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03686\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03687\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ EIGEN\_ARCH\_ARM64\ \&\&\ !EIGEN\_APPLE\_DOUBLE\_NEON\_BUG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03688\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03689\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ EIGEN\_COMP\_GNUC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03690\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Bug\ 907:\ workaround\ missing\ declarations\ of\ the\ following\ two\ functions\ in\ the\ ADK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03691\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Defining\ these\ functions\ as\ templates\ ensures\ that\ if\ these\ intrinsics\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03692\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ already\ defined\ in\ arm\_neon.h,\ then\ our\ workaround\ doesn't\ cause\ a\ conflict}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03693\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ has\ lower\ priority\ in\ overload\ resolution.}}
